                        <div data-reactid="876">
                         People love this property because is the best location and most delightful room in Whittier!!! The private room is on the first floor of an historic home built by the Briggs Family in 1901. Sleep in the comfort of an antique four-poster King-size bed with cozy linens and your own private toilet. We are in the nicest area of Uptown Whittier near Hadley St. on Bright Ave. Walk to dozens of cafe's, restaurants, bakeries, shops, theatre, museum, &amp; Whittier College. A perfect room for a travel nurse.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="877">
                         We made some recent changes in this listing to provide a more reasonable price for one or two travelers. The adjoining living room (Fairy Garden Room) is now only available by special request for an additional cost of $20 per person per day for up to two additional people (max is four people). The room has a king bed but we can fit an air bed on the floor in the room to accommodate up to three adults. Special rate for travel nurses: $42 per night for stays over 30 days. This includes the monthly cleaning fee. Please message me to get the special offer. The Briggs' King Suite is on the first floor of an elegant vintage modern Victorian home built in 1901. The space is shared with Grandmother Turtles' House, an historic home and mind, body, spirit healing facility in Uptown Whittier, CA. The Briggs' King Suite has a super comfortable four-poster King bed with designer bedding, piles of pillows, and an atmosphere of joyous relaxation. The room also has a private toilet and sink, which is rare in historic homes like this. We don't have a television but guests have access to FiOS Wifi so bring your own device. Spa Room and shower - The shower room is an old-fashioned "wet bathroom" that was remodeled in 2014 with pebble flooring and designer wood wall tiles from the floor to the 10-foot ceiling. Guests love the spa atmosphere, scrumptious soaps, and other spa essentials. The spa room is shared with other guests. Kitchenette - cozy but fully stocked with all the elements needed to prepare gourmet meals. Guests are welcome to use the tea kettle, skillet, wok, toaster oven, microwave, and use the dishes, utensils, and glassware but please clean up after yourself and do not leave dirty dishes anywhere. The kitchenette is shared with other guests. We are bicycle friendly but please leave your furry friends at home. A little history about the property: Grandmother Turtles' House is a product of divine intervention. The physical structure was built by one of the founding fathers of Whittier in 1901 when he and his family settled in the suburbs of downtown Los Angeles. The historic home was so badly damaged in the 1987 Whittier Narrows Earthquake that the owners sold it for $1 to anyone who wanted to save the house. To do so, they had to pick it up and move it! A counseling center purchased the property, moved it three lots away onto the current location, and rebuilt the structure to meet modern requirements. It was further updated in 2004 when a prominent local lawyer purchased the property. In late 2014, our family acquired it to create something. We were not sure exactly what or why we were so moved to buy this beautiful old house, but the drive was so deep and strong it could not be ignored. We named the property “Grandmother Turtles' House" to reflect the concept that the weight of the world is on Grandmother Turtle's back. The property is a place where people help other people. We are now a group of holistic practitioners, healers, and teachers on the journey to assist humanity to find purpose and love for themselves and others. Vacancies are rare for both of our guest rooms because of our location and wonderful accommodations. If you see availability, then we highly recommend to reserve the room or send me a message if you have questions.
                        </div>

                         Nestled against the Puente Hills Wildlife Preserve, historic Uptown Whittier Village is the heart of a charming thriving city filled with art, music, spirituality, exquisite cuisine, and culture. Our property is steps away from Greenleaf Avenue, Whittier College, the Community Center, Whittier History Museum, and the beautiful Puente Hills Preserve. We are centrally located between Disneyland and Universal Studios and about 30 minutes to the mountains, or to the beach, Los Angeles Staples Center, LA Fashion District, LA Convention Center, Seal Beach, etc., etc., etc…. Uptown Whittier is a wonderful busy place! The Uptown Whittier Organization has a handy compilation of restaurants, businesses, events, and other wonderful places to go and things to do in Uptown. Visit the Uptown Whittier Association website for more information.

                         Owner occupied (husband and wife) home. We do not have kids in our house. Looking for a Non-smoker, clean and organized home guests with no pets. House is located in one of the most sought after semi-private location in Cerritos.

                        <div data-reactid="2056">
                         Offers great privacy in the comfort of your own home complete with high-end professional appliances and furnishings, located in one of the safest cities in the United States that has tree lined middle roads and award winning schools, city library and auto square.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2057">
                         Semi-private neighborhood, most homes have outside security cameras. Quiet. Owner occupied (husband and wife) home. We do not have kids in our house. Looking for a Non-smoker, clean and organized home guest with no pets. House is located in one of the most sought after location in the city of Cerritos. This is a two story, 4 bedroom, 3 bath almost 3,000 sq. ft. home with two car garage and driveway for up to three vehicles. We have two refrigerators (one in the garage). Fully furnished professional gourmet Kitchen. Washer and dryer for laundry in the garage. Internet and Direct TV satellite provided. Nice front patio and huge backyard landscaped garden. This home was a former recipient of Cerritos House of the Year award. Located in a quiet and friendly neighborhood of Cerritos, which is one of the safest cities in the country and is within the best school district in the L.A. county. Walking distance to Cerritos Town Center, restaurants and groceries. Average neighborhood home in the area is typically valued way over $800K.
                        </div>
